### BREAKING CHANGES

* @morfeo/core: breaking change the the core api:

1. morfeo.useTheme renamed into morfeo.setCurrentTheme
2. morfeo.getCurrent renamed into morfeo.getCurrentTheme

### BREAKING CHANGES

* @morfeo/core: breaking change the the core api:

1. morfeo.useTheme renamed into morfeo.setCurrentTheme
2. morfeo.getCurrent renamed into morfeo.getCurrentTheme
